   <!-- looking for GDPR cookie -->
   <script>
    function cookieClose() {
         setCookie('cookie_acknowlege', 'true', 3650);
     }
 
     function hideCookieContainer() {
         var el = document.getElementById('cookie-row');
         el.className += " hide";
     }
 
     function setCookie(name, value, days) {
         var expires = "";
         if (days) {
             var date = new Date();
             date.setTime(date.getTime() + (days * 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000));
             expires = "; expires=" + date.toUTCString();
         }
 
         document.cookie = name + "=" + (value || "") + expires + "; path=/";
         hideCookieContainer();
     }
 
     function getCookie(name) {
         var dc = document.cookie;
         var prefix = name + "=";
         var begin = dc.indexOf("; " + prefix);
         if (begin == -1) {
             begin = dc.indexOf(prefix);
             if (begin != 0) return null;
         } else {
             begin += 2;
             var end = document.cookie.indexOf(";", begin);
             if (end == -1) {
                 end = dc.length;
             }
         }
 
         // because unescape has been deprecated, replaced with decodeURI
         //return unescape(dc.substring(begin + prefix.length, end));
         return decodeURI(dc.substring(begin + prefix.length, end));
     }
   </script>
   <style>
    /* GDPR START*/

         right: 0;
         color: #fff;
         font-weight: 300;
         text-align: center;

     }

     }

             color: #FFF;
         }
 
     .cookie-row p .learn_more {
         color: #FFF !important;
     }
 
     .cookie-row a, .cookie-row a:visited {
         text-decoration: underline;

     }

   <script>
    $(document).ready(function () {
 
         var nofollow = $(".no-follow-versatag a");
         $("a[href]")
             .not(".no-follow-versatag, [href='#'], [href=''], .versaTagConditional, .versaTagiOS, .versaTagAndroid")
             .not(nofollow);
 
         $("form,form:not(#travelguide)").submit(function (ev) {
             versaTagObj.generateRequest(ev.currentTarget.action);
         });
 
         $(".versaTagConditional").click(function () {
             var ebMailPacket = document.getElementById("mail");
             var ebViewOnline = document.getElementById("online");
 
             if (ebMailPacket.checked) {
                 versaTagObj.generateRequest("https://www.traveltex.com/versaTag/guide_order_confirmation.html");
             } if (ebViewOnline.checked) {
                 versaTagObj.generateRequest("https://www.traveltex.com/versaTag/view_travel_guide.html");
             }
         });
 
         $(".versaTagiOS").click(function () {
             versaTagObj.generateRequest("https://www.traveltex.com/VERSATAGios");
         });
 
         $(".versaTagAndroid").click(function () {
             versaTagObj.generateRequest("https://www.traveltex.com/VERSATAGandroid");
         });
     });
   </script>

   <script type="text/javascript">
    $(function () {
             $('a[href*=#]:not([href=#])').click(function () {
                 if (location.pathname.replace(/^\//, '') == this.pathname.replace(/^\//, '') && location.hostname == this.hostname) {
                     var target = $(this.hash);
                     target = target.length ? target : $('[name=' + this.hash.slice(1) + ']');
                     if (target.length) {
                         $('html,body').animate({
                             scrollTop: target.offset().top
                         }, 1000);
                         return false;
                     }
                 }
             });
         });
   </script>
